2. The price of the hotel matches the corresponding grade. The price in the off-season is affordable, but the premium in the peak season is up to you.
3. The hotel is quiet and far away from the downtown area, so you don‚Äôt need to drive or take a taxi when traveling.
4. If you have high reflexes, the hotel also provides soothing health products.
Several discrepancies/disadvantages:
1. No room upgrades were arranged during the off-season. I chose not the lowest room type, but there was no upgrade. The reception at the front desk was slightly inflexible.
2. The housekeeping service is not adequate, the room card fails, and I have to travel far to replace it myself. The reply was that you can go to the foot of the mountain for normal activities and there are no special arrangements.
3. The variety of breakfast is lower than expected and relatively simple. It is recommended to start breakfast as early as seven o'clock.

msg:The hotel on the second day of my trip to Dali. Compared with the Qinhai B&B in Shuanglang Erhai, Yiyun Hotel seems more mature and stable. The online reviews are indeed correct. Parents and elders must be very satisfied with this hotel.

The location is near the ancient city of Dali. It takes a short drive up the mountain. It takes about fifteen minutes from the ancient city.

We booked a private hot spring room type and were very satisfied. Compared with the ordinary courtyard view room, the private hot spring room was so comfortable. Especially after a week's journey, the constant temperature private hot spring bath made our body recover a lot. We spent the night and the second day. I took a bath every morning and it was very private.

The smart curtains and screens throughout the house are very nice and provide a great experience.

In terms of food, the afternoon tea was very good and delicious. For breakfast the next day, the hotel allowed our family of three to choose all the breakfasts we wanted to eat. There were many varieties and they were all wrapped in plastic wrap, which was very hygienic. The stewed wontons and fried dough sticks tasted a little average, but everything else was good.

Before departure the next day, we also took a walk in the hotel park. The environment was still very good. The only drawback may be the lack of some public entertainment areas.
